## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Findings: Grafana Alerting Go Source Files

### 1. Legacy Alerting Engine
The legacy alerting engine runtime has been **fully removed** from this version of Grafana (no `pkg/services/alerting/` directory exists). Only the database schema definition remains:

| File | Role |
|------|------|
| `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/alert_mig.go` | Defines the SQL schema for the legacy `alert` table (dashboard-based alert rules), `alert_rule_tag`, `alert_notification`, and `alert_notification_state` tables |

---

### 2. Unified Alerting (ngalert) Engine
| File | Role |
|------|------|
| `pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go` | Main `AlertNG` service entry point — wires scheduler, evaluator, notifier, state manager, API, and store |
| `pkg/services/ngalert/store/alert_rule.go` | Core CRUD for unified alert rules against the `alert_rule` / `alert_rule_version` tables (`InsertAlertRules`, `UpdateAlertRules`, `ListAlertRules`, `GetAlertRulesKeysForScheduling`, etc.) |
| `pkg/services/ngalert/store/database.go` | Defines `DBstore` struct, `AlertingStore` interface, and `ProvideDBStore` constructor |
| `pkg/services/ngalert/models/alert_rule.go` | `AlertRule` model + migration label constants (`MigratedLabelPrefix = "__legacy_"`, `MigratedUseLegacyChannelsLabel`, `MigratedContactLabelPrefix`, etc.) |
| `pkg/services/ngalert/store/instance_database.go` | Alert instance (firing state) storage in `alert_instance` table |
| `pkg/services/ngalert/store/alertmanager.go` | Alertmanager configuration storage in `alert_configuration` / `alert_configuration_history` |
| `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/` | Alert rule scheduler and evaluator |
